GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_t*sin(log(A + c3))
Candidates evaluated: 50

I need to check if any candidate can exactly match the ground truth:

**GT:** `-0.4537*A*exp(-0.08462*t) + 0.7535*sin(log(A + 1))`

The GT has two fundamentally different basis functions:
1. `A*exp(-αt)` — a product of A and a decaying exponential in t
2. `sin(log(A+1))` — a sine of a logarithm

Let me analyze the candidates systematically, focusing on whether they contain the necessary basis functions.

**Key observation:** The term `sin(log(A+1))` is a very specific nonlinear function of A. Most candidates use combinations of polynomials in A, exponentials in A, logarithms, rational functions, tanh, etc. None of these can produce `sin(log(A+1))` exactly.

Similarly, `A*exp(-αt)` requires a product of A with an exponential in t. Many candidates have `exp(c*t)` terms but not multiplied by A.

Let me check candidates that contain `sin`:

**Candidate 30:** `c0*tanh(c1*t+c2) + c3*sin(A*c4+c5) + c6 + t/(A*c7+c8)`
- Has `sin(A*c4+c5)` — this is sin of a linear function of A, NOT sin(log(A+1)). These are fundamentally different functions. No match.

**Candidate 37:** `A*c0*tanh(c1*t+c2) + c3*sin(A*c4+c5) + ...`
- Same issue: `sin(linear in A)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`. No match.

**Candidate 40:** `A*c0 + c1*tanh(c2*t+c3) + c4 + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + t/(A*c8+c9)`
- Same: `sin(linear in A)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`. No match.

Now let me check candidates with `log` terms that might combine with other functions:

**Candidate 10:** `A^c0*c1 + c2/(c3+c4*exp(c5*t)) + c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8*log(A*c9+1)`
- Has `log(A+1)` terms but not `sin(log(A+1))`. Log ≠ sin(log). No match.

**Candidate 27:** Contains `A^c0` and `log(A*c7+1)` terms divided by sigmoid-like expressions. No sin(log) term. No match.

**Candidate 43:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2 + c3 + c4/(c5+c6*exp(c7*t)) + c8*log(A*c9+1)`
- Has log but not sin(log). No match.

**Candidate 44:** `A^c0*c1 + c2/(c3+c4*exp(c5*t)) + c6*exp(A*c7) + c8*log(A*c9+1)`
- Has log but not sin(log). No match.

**Systematic check:** The GT requires `sin(log(A+1))` as a basis function. This is a transcendental function that cannot be expressed as any combination of:
- Polynomials in A
- exp(A), exp(t)
- log(A+1) (without sin)
- tanh
- Rational functions
- A^c (power functions)
- sin(linear in A) (which is different from sin(log(A+1)))

None of the 50 candidates contain `sin(log(...))` as a component. The only candidates with `sin` are 30, 37, and 40, and they all have `sin(linear function of A)`, which is fundamentally different from `sin(log(A+1))`.

Since `sin(log(A+1))` is linearly independent from all basis functions present in any candidate, and it has a non-zero coefficient (0.7535) in the GT, no candidate can match.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK12)

GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_t*sin(log(A + c3))

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.4537*A*exp(-0.08462*t) + 0.7535*sin(log(A + 1))`

The GT has two terms:
1. `A*exp(-c*t)` — a product of A and a decaying exponential in t
2. `sin(log(A + 1))` — a sine of logarithm function of A only

Key basis functions in GT: `A*exp(t)` type term and `sin(log(A+1))`.

Let me analyze each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

**Critical observation:** The GT contains `sin(log(A + 1))`, which is a very specific nonlinear function. No combination of polynomials, exponentials, tanh, rational functions, or power functions can reproduce `sin(log(A+1))` exactly. Only candidates containing `sin(log(...))` or equivalent can match.

Let me scan all candidates for `sin(log(...))`:
- None of the candidates contain `sin(log(...))`.

Let me check for `log` combined with `sin`:
- Candidates with `sin`: 30, 37, 40 — these have `sin(A*c4 + c5)` which is `sin` of a linear function of A, not `sin(log(A+1))`.
- Candidates with `log`: 10, 24, 27, 28, 34-36, 38, 41-46, 48, 43, 44 — these have `log` but not inside `sin`.

**No candidate has `sin(log(...))`.**

Since `sin(log(A+1))` cannot be expressed as any combination of:
- Polynomials in A
- `exp(c*A)` 
- `A^c` (power functions)
- `tanh(...)` 
- `log(A+1)` (without sin)
- `sin(c*A + d)` (sin of linear, not log)
- Rational functions of A
- `1/A`, `sqrt(A+c)`, etc.

These are all linearly independent basis functions. The function `sin(log(A+1))` is fundamentally different from all of these.

Let me verify: Could `sin(log(A+1))` be approximated by any of these? No — we need EXACT equivalence, not approximation. By the linear independence principle (Rule 3), `sin(log(A+1))` cannot be exactly represented by any finite combination of the basis functions present in the candidates.

Therefore, **no candidate can match the GT**.

Let me do a quick double-check on candidates with `sin`:
- **Candidate 30:** `c0*tanh(c1*t+c2) + c3*sin(A*c4+c5) + c6 + t/(A*c7+c8)` — has `sin(c4*A + c5)`, not `sin(log(A+1))`. These are different functions.
- **Candidate 37:** `A*c0*tanh(...) + c3*sin(A*c4+c5) + ...` — same issue.
- **Candidate 40:** `... + c5*sin(A*c6+c7) + ...` — same issue.

`sin(c*A)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))` for any constant c, as the arguments are fundamentally different functions.
